msg:Very nice hotel. Staff was very helpful and polite, though was offered an upgrade like many of the other reviewers I've seen (but not a negative). Pool is very small and a bit of a mess, it is open to the community and the locker room is a bit rundown and it was too crowded to enjoy during my entire stay. The rooms are very nice and clean and the lobby and communal spaces are very nice. 24hr room service is a big plus. The layout of the lobby on the 3rd floor without direct elevator access to the 1st floor is annoying. All deliveries have to be met at the 1st floor and that requires going all the way through the lobby on the 3rd floor and either taking another elevator or two flights of escalators to receive.

msg:Come to hand in homework, it's been delayed for a long time
During the seven-day trip to Beijing, I stayed in three hotels. The first Beijing Conference Center was not open to the public. It was booked by the organizer. I thought it was hopeless, but I didn’t expect to find that not only the room size is large, but the service is also good.
The second hotel is Hilton, and the third is Jinling Hotel. Because I live in Nanjing, I have a good impression of Jinling Hotel.
Let’s compare Metropark and Jinling Hotel:
Both are upgraded for free. On the first night, both prices are the same.
Room size: Jinling is larger than Metropark, and the air in the room tastes better than Jinling. Metropark has a small bay window sill, and a tea table is arranged. You can make tea before going out and when you come back at night, so as to relieve the greasyness of eating Peking duck. This is good. The quality of the tea is too poor, you can bring your own tea.
Jinling Hotel has a staff member who added me to WeChat, and the service is more considerate, including that I was playing outside and couldn’t make it back to check out. If it was delayed, the staff would help me pack it up and put it in the luggage storage
Takeaway: Jinling Hotel can be delivered to the door of the room for free, and it is delivered by a robot, which the children like very much; Metropark has to go over the mountains and mountains by itself, get dressed and come down to get it
Continued stay: Metropark increases the fare by 200 yuan, and Jinling hardly increases the fare. This feels very important, haha

❇️The hotel is magnificent and the lobby is huge. Because the shape of the hotel is relatively irregular, so are the rooms. The room is a good size and the bathroom is also a good size. The overall level of hardware facilities is above average. It's quite comfortable to live in.

I hope my review can sound the alarm for hotel services and face up to hygiene issues, because no matter how many stars the hotel ranks One is always hygiene.

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Business travelers
info:1 Review
rating:1
posted:Posted July 16, 2023
msg:本來要住三天，住到第二天直接退訂，
夜裡回到酒店已經極其勞累，直接躺下，半夜一直有光閃爍，以為閃電，後發現是燈光一直閃爍，本來想聯繫換房間，但酒店電話打不通。不想起來下樓，就想忍受一下，幾小時就要起來工作。隨後空調不斷重啟，噪音很大，反覆起來重新插拔取電卡，每次弄完會有不一樣的燈閃爍。直至床頭的閲讀燈也開始不斷頻閃，才終於無法忍受從網上找了酒店電話，聯繫酒店來維修，此時房間所有開關都失效。檢查後説是酒店的取電系統壞了，等着維修完已經6點，距離出去工作衹有一小時。

和前台溝通，值班經理態度好，其他也算還行，應該有3分以上，但酒店的決策層用0分不足以形容。所以衹能所有是最低分。一夜沒有睡好，造成第二天連續工作了41小時。酒店所謂“領導”表示，以後再來可以升級房型。後來表示可以退30%，表示不滿意後又表示可以退50%。一共住三天，我沒有因為失去一個晚上的睡眠第二天要連軸工作而要求賠償，但這一夜的設備故障造成客人完全沒有休息，是不是退這一天款是基本禮貌。我不知是覺得客人太好糊弄麼。之前公司出差都是住這裏，以後會要求自己公司所有人出差不允許選擇這裏。可能酒店生意好，不在乎，但我會做自己所能做的。

不知誰決策的，因為幾百塊，而失去服務行業的基本態度，格局可以。
再次感謝前台經理的爭取，感受到她面對不公的無能為力

用品擺放侷促，且沒有浴缸，不符合酒店定位！

大堂裝飾裝潢很漂亮，很喜歡
整體環境香氛很平和耐聞。

預訂的時候下了兩份早餐，
前台沒認真核對就説房間不含早餐，後又更正

早餐廳存在一些不合理
1.進門無法第一位置拿到盤子，盤子在第一個熱菜區下方，如遇上用餐高峯取餐盤要等別人盛完菜才能拿略顯尷尬。

2.進門首先看見和經過的是塑料盒裝酸奶區，有點奇怪
3.用餐非高峯期，收餐人員推着泔水車在用餐區流動打掃，給人感覺很不好
4.餐具直接放在桌墊上，衞生和審美都不妥
5.餐具中缺少餐刀，與早餐風格和性質不配套，黃油衹能拿勺子抹

早餐廳師傅態度都很好，服務意識良好，有一款肉桂香的麪包烤的很好，值得肯定！
